decouple	At the moment when the virus first started to spread in Wuhan last year, America’s tariff rate on imports was back to its highest level since 1993 and both America and China had begun to Word?</span><span class="body"><span class="h1">agenda / diary / schedule / timetable </span><span class="bullet"><span class="li"> A book with a space for each day where you write down things that you have to do in the future is called a <span class="eb">diary</span> or a <span class="eb">datebook</span> <span class="label-g"><span class="wrap">(</span><span class="geo" geo="n_am">North American English</span><span class="wrap">)</span></span> (not an <span class="ei">agenda</span>). You may also have a <span class="eb">calendar</span> on your desk or hanging up in your room, where you write down your appointments. A <span class="eb">diary</span> or a <span class="eb">journal</span> is also the record that some people keep of what has happened during the day:<span class="x-gs"><span class="x-g"><span class="x">The Diary of Anne Frank</span></span></span>.</span><span class="li"> In <span class="label-g"><span class="geo" geo="br">British English</span></span> your <span class="eb">schedule</span> is a plan that lists all the work that you have to do and when you must do each thing and a <span class="eb">timetable</span> is a list showing the fixed times at which events will happen:<span class="x-gs"><span class="x-g"><span class="x">a bus/​train timetable</span></span></span>. In <span class="label-g"><span class="geo" geo="n_am">North American English</span></span> these are both called a <span class="eb">schedule</span>.</span></span></span></span></span></li><li class="sn-g"><a href="entry://#97623b3cbaa743ec9120199080f55335" class="sen"></a><span class="num">3</span><span class="def">the intention behind what somebody says or does, that is often secret</span><span class="x-gs"><span class="x-g"> <span class="rx-g"><span class="x">The artist is letting <span class="cl"><strong>his own agenda</strong></span> affect what was meant to be a community project.</span></span></span></span> <span class="xr-gs"><span class="prefix">see also</span> <a class="Ref" href="entry://hidden agenda" otitle="hidden agenda definition"><span class="xr-g"><span class="xh">hidden agenda</span></span></a></span></li></span> <span class="res-g"><span class="collapse" otitle="Word Origin"><span class="unbox is-active"> <span class="heading" onclick="if(this.parentNode.className=='unbox'){this.parentNode.className='unbox is-active';}else if(this.parentNode.className=='unbox is-active'){this.parentNode.className='unbox';}">Word Origin</span><span class="body"> <span class="def">early 17th cent.</span> (in the sense <span class="qt">‘things to be done’</span>): from <span class="lang">Latin</span>, neuter plural of <span class="ff">agendum</span>, gerundive of <span class="ff">agere</span> ‘do’.</span></span></span><span class="collapse" otitle="Extra examples"><span class="unbox"><span class="heading" class="row vg-header"><div class="col"><h2>Definition of <em>lockdown</em></h2><p class="entryNumbers"></p></div></div> <div class="vg"><div class="sb has-num"><span class="sb-0"><div class="sense has-num-only"><span class="sn sense-1"><span class="num">1</span></span> <span class="dt"><span class="dtText"><strong class="mw_t_bc">: </strong>the confinement of prisoners to their cells for all or most of the day as a temporary security measure</span></span></div></span></div> <div class="sb has-num has-let"><span class="sb-0"><div class="sense has-sn"><span class="sn sense-2 a"><span class="num">2</span><span class="letter">a</span></span> <span class="dt"><span class="dtText"><strong class="mw_t_bc">: </strong>an emergency measure or condition in which people are temporarily prevented from entering or leaving a restricted area or building (such as a school) during a threat of danger                                                                <span class="ex-sent first-child t has-aq sents">… the school went on <span class="mw_t_wi">lockdown</span> when a student brought a pellet gun to campus.</span><span class="ex-sent aq has-aq sents"><span class="aq"><span class="auth">— Ian Gordon</span></span></span></span></span></div></span> <span class="sb-1"><div class="sense has-sn"><span class="sn sense-b"><span class="letter">b</span></span> <span class="dt"><span class="dtText"><strong class="mw_t_bc">: </strong>a temporary condition imposed by governmental authorities (as during the outbreak of an epidemic disease) in which people are required to stay in their homes and refrain from or limit activities outside the home involving public contact (such as dining out or attending large gatherings)                                                                <span class="ex-sent first-child t has-aq sents">Authorities placed the central Chinese city under <span class="mw_t_wi">lockdown</span> on Jan. 23 after the virus had infected hundreds of residents and was just starting its spread across the globe.</span><span class="ex-sent aq has-aq sents"><span class="aq"><span class="auth">— Darryl Coote</span></span> <span class="ex-sent t has-aq sents">The San Francisco Bay Area <span class="mw_t_wi">lockdown</span> and national guidelines signal a rapid escalation of government and business efforts to halt the coronavirus spread via restrictions that will slam the brakes on economic activity.</span><span class="ex-sent aq has-aq sents"><span class="aq"><span class="auth">— Ed Carson</span></span> <p class="snote"><span class="note-txt">Note:</span>            Individuals who are employed in various occupational fields (such as healthcare, public works, law enforcement, and food supply) considered essential to public health and safety may continue working outside the home during a lockdown.      </p></span></span></span></span></div></span></div></div></div> <span id="anchor-seporator"></span>
